     function setAttributeOnload(object, attribute, val) {
      if(window.addEventListener) {
        window.addEventListener('load',

      } else {

         <script>
          function startHide(page) {
	if (!requestURIContains(page)) {
		document.write('&lt;p&gt;&lt;small class="readmore" onclick="window.location.href=\'' + page + '\';"&gt;Click here to read the entire article ..&lt;/small&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div style="display: none;"&gt;');
		var divs = document.getElementsByTagName('div');
		for (var i = 0; i &lt; divs.length; i++) {
			if (divs[i].id == 'fastmenu') {
				divs[i].style.display = 'none';
			}
		}
	}
}
function endHide(page) {
	if (!requestURIContains(page)) {
		document.write('&lt;/div&gt;');
	}
}
function requestURIContains(part) {
	return window.location.href.toLowerCase().indexOf(part) &gt; -1;
}
         </script>
        </div>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>

             </a>
             <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
              Using datatables
             </h3>
             <div class="post-header">
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="post-body entry-content">
              <div style="border: 3px red double; padding: 3px; background: #ffc;">
               <h4>
                WARNING - OUTDATED CONTENT!
               </h4>
               <p>
                This article is targeted on JSF 1.2. For JSF 2.0, using datatables can be approached much more elegantly with help of a
                <code>
                 @ViewScoped
                </code>
                managed bean. Please checkout
                <a href="http://balusc.blogspot.com/2010/06/benefits-and-pitfalls-of-viewscoped.html">
                 this article
                </a>
                which contains two basic CRUD examples, one for JSF 2.0 on Servlet 2.5 and other for JSF 2.0 on Servlet 3.0 which supports passing method arguments in EL 2.2.
               </p>
              </div>
              <div id="fastmenu">
               <select onchange="document.location.href = this.options[this.selectedIndex].value">
                <option value="">
                 Fast menu
                </option>
                <option value="#CreateDTOClass">

                </option>
                <option value="#RetrieveAndStoreData">

                </option>
                <option value="#ShowDataContentsInDatatable">
                 Show data contents in datatable
                </option>

                 Add backing bean action to every row
                </option>
                <option value="#GetSelectedDatatableRow">
                 Get selected datatable row
                </option>
                <option value="#ShowSelectedDataItem">
                 Show selected data item
                </option>
                <option value="#SaveEditedDataItem">
                 Save edited data item
                </option>

                </option>

                </option>

              <h4>
               Introduction
              </h4>
              <p>
               This whole JSF datatable howto is based on the use of a backing bean with the
               <b>
                request
               </b>
               scope. You can use it in a session scoped bean, but you have to do some finetuning and those will be explained in the text. It's recommended to use
               <b>
                at least
               </b>
               <a href="https://javaserverfaces.dev.java.net/" target="_blank">
                JSF RI 1.1_02
               </a>
               or
               <a href="https://javaserverfaces.dev.java.net/" target="_blank">
                JSF RI 1.2_02
               </a>
               (and thus not 1.x_01 or older; newer is always better, pick the newest if you can), because the 1.x_02 has some important bugfixes. The code examples given below are based on JSF RI 1.2 (Mojarra) with at least Java EE 5.0. At the bottom of this article you can
               <a href="#DownloadWAR">
                download
               </a>
               a WAR containing all examples in Request as well as Session scope using Sun JSF Mojarra 1.2.
              </p>
              <script>
               startHide('/2006/06/using-datatables.html');
              </script>
              <h4>
               <a href="#CreateDTOClass" name="CreateDTOClass">
                Create DTO class
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               The
               <span class="code">
                h:dataTable
               </span>
               dynamic tables are nice, you can put any
               <span class="code">
                <a href="http://java.sun.com/j2se/1.5.0/docs/api/java/util/List.html" target="_blank">
                 List
                </a>
               </span>
               or
               <span class="code">
                <a href="http://java.sun.com/javaee/javaserverfaces/1.2/docs/api/javax/faces/model/DataModel.html" target="_blank">
                 DataModel
                </a>
               </span>
               of DTO or
               <span class="code">
                <a href="http://java.sun.com/j2se/1.5.0/docs/api/java/util/Map.html" target="_blank">
                 Map
                </a>
               </span>
               objects in it. In this article we'll use a List of DTO's.
              </p>
              <p>
               Imagine a SQL database containing a table with three fields: ID, Name and Value. First create a data wrapper class which represents each single row of the table, this is just a simple class with the table fields (columns) definied as encapsulated private variables which can be accessed by public getters and setters. Such a class is also known as a DTO (Data Transfer Object).
              </p>
              <p>
               Here is an example called
               <b>
                MyData.java
               </b>
               :
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mymodel;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyData {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               Long
               <span class="codeproperty">
                id
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               String
               <span class="codeproperty">
                name
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               String
               <span class="codeproperty">
                value
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               Long getId() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                id
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String getName() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                name
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String getValue() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                value
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Setters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setId(Long id) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                id
               </span>
               = id;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setName(String name) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                name
               </span>
               = name;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setValue(String value) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                value
               </span>
               = value;
    }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               It's a good practice to use wrapper datatype objects (
               <span class="code">
                Long
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="code">
                Boolean
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="code">
                Integer
               </span>
               , etc) instead of primitive datatypes (
               <span class="codekeyword">
                long
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                boolean
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               , etc) for the properties, because the database fields can contain null values which can not be put into a primitive at all.
              </p>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#RetrieveAndStoreData" name="RetrieveAndStoreData">
                Retrieve and store data
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You can use
               <a href="http://www.hibernate.org" target="_blank">
                Hibernate
               </a>
               or just plain
               <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_Database_Connectivity" target="_blank">
                JDBC
               </a>
               to retrieve SQL data. It must return a
               <span class="code">
                List
               </span>
               of
               <span class="code">
                MyData
               </span>
               objects. This has to be stored in a private variable
               <span class="code">
                dataList
               </span>
               which can be accessed by a getter and setter. The setter of the
               <span class="code">
                dataList
               </span>
               is actually not used by JSF pages (only UIInput values require setters). You can safely remove it if you don't use it somewhere else in the backing bean logic.
              </p>
              <p>
               The data layer and the DAO pattern is explained in this tutorial:
               <a href="http://balusc.blogspot.com/2008/07/dao-tutorial-data-layer.html" target="_blank">
                DAO tutorial - the data layer
               </a>
               .
              </p>
              <p>
               Here is the relevant java code for the backing bean. You can load the
               <span class="code">
                dataList
               </span>
               in either the constructor
               <b>
                or
               </b>
               initialization block of the bean:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.List;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.context.FacesContext;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               mydao.DAOException;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               mydao.DAOFactory;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               mydao.MyDataDAO;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               mymodel.MyData;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               MyDataDAO
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataDAO
               </span>
               = DAOFactory.getInstance(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "javabase"
               </span>
               ).getMyDataDAO();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt;
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ;

    {
        loadDataList();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Preload in initialization block.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Constructor -------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               MyBean() {
        loadDataList();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // OR preload in constructor.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               loadDataList() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Do your "SELECT * FROM mydata" thing.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                try
               </span>
               {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataDAO
               </span>
               .list();
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                catch
               </span>
               (DAOException e) {
            setErrorMessage(e.getMessage() +
               <span class="codevalue">
                " Cause: "
               </span>
               + e.getCause());
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt; getDataList() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ;
    }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               If you're going to use this bean for other purposes than only showing the datalist, then you can better move the loading to the getter so that the data won't be loaded everytime when the bean is constructed. Also use
               <i>
                lazy loading
               </i>
               in the getter so that the data won't be loaded everytime when the getter is called during the bean's life. Here is an example:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt; getDataList() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ==
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) {
            loadDataList();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Preload by lazy loading.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ;
    }
              </pre>
              <p>
               <b>
                Session scope:
               </b>
               once loaded the
               <span class="code">
                dataList
               </span>
               will persist during the session and won't be garbaged after one request in the same session. If you want to reload the session data every view to get the most recent data, then do as follows:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt; getDataList() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (FacesContext.getCurrentInstance().getRenderResponse()) {
            loadDataList();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Reload to get most recent data.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ;
    }
              </pre>
              <p>
               The
               <span class="code">
                FacesContext#getRenderResponse()
               </span>
               returns
               <span class="codekeyword">
                true
               </span>
               when this getter is invoked during the render response phase. This is to prevent duplicate reloads as this getter can also be invoked during the apply request values phase or the process validations phase. Also see
               <a href="/2006/09/debug-jsf-lifecycle.html">
                Debug JSF lifecycle
               </a>
               .
              </p>
              <p>
               You can also consider to use two beans: one request-scoped bean for the views and form actions and one session-scoped bean for the session data. You can inject the session scoped bean in the request scoped bean as managed property using faces-config.xml. And in the request scoped bean you can invoke reload of the data after save/update/delete action of the session data. Also see
               <a href="/2006/06/communication-in-jsf.html">
                Communication in JSF
               </a>
               .
              </p>
              <p>
               Storing the data in the session scope has not only an impact on the server memory usage, but also on the user experience when the data is not for display only. Imagine what would happen with the data when the user manages (edit/delete) the data in multiple browser windows/tabs in the same session.
              </p>
              <p>
               Instead of using the session scope you can also consider using the Tomahawk
               <span class="code">
                t:dataTable
               </span>
               component. It has an extra attribute '
               <span clas="code">
                preserveDataModel
               </span>
               ' which you should set to true. This will store the datatable value in the component tree state in session and restore it during the next request. This way you can also avoid unforeseen concurrent updates on the datamodel in between the requests.
              </p>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#ShowDataContentsInDatatable" name="ShowDataContentsInDatatable">
                Show data contents in datatable
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               First define the backing bean as a request scoped managed bean
               <span class="code">
                myBean
               </span>
               in the
               <b>
                faces-config.xml
               </b>
               .
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;managed-bean&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;managed-bean-name&gt;
               </span>
               myBean
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/managed-bean-name&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;managed-bean-class&gt;
               </span>
               mypackage.MyBean
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/managed-bean-class&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;managed-bean-scope&gt;
               </span>
               request
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/managed-bean-scope&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/managed-bean&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               <b>
                Session scope:
               </b>
               if you want to use the session scope, just change
               <span class="code">
                request
               </span>
               to
               <span class="code">
                session
               </span>
               .
              </p>
              <p>
               Now you can use the
               <span class="code">
                h:dataTable
               </span>
               to show the contents of the retrieved list.
              </p>
              <p>
               The relevant JSF code looks like:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.name}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.value}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               The
               <span class="code">
                h:dataTable value
               </span>
               should contain the retrieved list from the backing bean definied as managed bean
               <span class="code">
                myBean
               </span>
               . The
               <span class="code">
                h:dataTable var
               </span>
               is just a holder for every MyData object of the list. This can be used to access the getters and setters of MyData.java.
              </p>
              <p>
               The
               <span class="code">
                f:facet
               </span>
               components are optional. In this case the
               <span class="code">
                f:facet name="header"
               </span>
               represents the table header (in HTML terms, the &lt;th&gt; element). If you don't need it, you can just leave it away.
              </p>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#AddBackingBeanActionToEveryRow" name="AddBackingBeanActionToEveryRow">
                Add backing bean action to every row
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You can use
               <span class="code">
                h:commandLink
               </span>
               or
               <span class="code">
                h:commandButton
               </span>
               in one or more columns to invoke a backing bean action and pass the appropriate MyData object to MyBean. This is faster than passing a
               <span class="code">
                <a href="/2006/06/communication-in-jsf.html">
                 f:attribute
                </a>
               </span>
               tag with an ID to retrieve the selected item by ID straight from the database. To get the selected row, use the
               <span class="code">
                h:dataTable binding
               </span>
               to dynamically bind the state of the datatable to the backing bean, so that it knows which row was clicked.
              </p>
              <p>
               Update the JSP as follows:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               binding=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataTable}"
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandLink
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id}"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.editDataItem}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               Another way is using
               <span class="code">
                f:setPropertyActionListener
               </span>
               to set the currently iterated MyData object as a property of MyBean.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandLink
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id}"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.editDataItem}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:setPropertyActionListener
               </span>
               target=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataItem}"
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:commandLink&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#GetSelectedDatatableRow" name="GetSelectedDatatableRow">
                Get selected datatable row
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               Clicking at the
               <span class="code">
                h:commandLink
               </span>
               of every row will invoke the
               <span class="code">
                editDataItem()
               </span>
               method of the backing bean. The MyData item belonging to the row can be retrieved using the
               <span class="code">
                getRowData()
               </span>
               method of the
               <span class="code">
                <a href="http://java.sun.com/javaee/javaserverfaces/1.2/docs/api/javax/faces/component/html/HtmlDataTable.html" target="_blank">
                 HtmlDataTable
                </a>
               </span>
               class, which is bound by
               <span class="code">
                h:dataTable binding
               </span>
               . Finally store the MyData item as
               <span class="code">
                dataItem
               </span>
               .
              </p>
              <p>
               As we aren't going to make the ID of the MyData item editable, we need to store its value in a
               <span class="code">
                HtmlInputHidden
               </span>
               component bound to the page so that it can be retained in the next request, even if the validation phase fails.
              </p>
              <p>
               So extend the backing bean with the following code to retrieve the MyData item of the row selected:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlDataTable;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlInputHidden;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               mymodel.MyData;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               HtmlDataTable
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               MyData
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               MyData();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               HtmlInputHidden
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItemId
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlInputHidden();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String editDataItem() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Get selected MyData item to be edited.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               = (MyData) dataTable.getRowData();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Store the ID of the data item in hidden input element.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItemId
               </span>
               .setValue(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               .getId());
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codevalue">
                "edit"
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Navigation case.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               HtmlDataTable getDataTable() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               MyData getDataItem() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               HtmlInputHidden getDataItemId() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItemId
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Setters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setDataTable(HtmlDataTable dataTable) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               = dataTable;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setDataItem(MyData dataItem) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               = dataItem;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setDataItemId(HtmlInputHidden dataItemId) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItemId
               </span>
               = dataItemId;
    }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               <b>
                Session scope:
               </b>
               you don't need to pre-instantiate the
               <span class="code">
                dataItem
               </span>
               with
               <span class="code">
                <span class="codekeyword">
                 new
                </span>
                MyData()
               </span>
               as this won't be garbaged after one request. That same way you don't need to retain the ID of the MyData item, so you can safely remove the
               <span class="code">
                dataItemId
               </span>
               property along with all related logic.
              </p>
              <p>
               When you're using the
               <span class="code">
                f:setPropertyActionListner
               </span>
               approach, then the backing bean class should rather look like:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlInputHidden;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               mymodel.MyData;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               MyData
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               HtmlInputHidden
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItemId
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlInputHidden();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String editDataItem() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // The dataItem is already set by f:setPropertyActionListener.
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Store the ID of the data item in hidden input element.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItemId
               </span>
               .setValue(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               .getId());
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codevalue">
                "edit"
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Navigation case.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               MyData getDataItem() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               HtmlInputHidden getDataItemId() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItemId
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Setters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setDataItem(MyData dataItem) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               = dataItem;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setDataItemId(HtmlInputHidden dataItemId) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItemId
               </span>
               = dataItemId;
    }

}
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#ShowSelectedDataItem" name="ShowSelectedDataItem">
                Show selected data item
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               The contents of the MyData item retrieved can be shown in a new JSP file for edit or just for view. In this example we will show the item for edit.
              </p>
              <p>
               The relevant JSF code:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:panelGrid
               </span>
               columns=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "2"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataItem.id}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:inputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataItem.name}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:inputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataItem.value}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:panelGrid&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:inputHidden
               </span>
               binding=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataItemId}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Save"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.saveDataItem}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               <b>
                Session scope:
               </b>
               as mentioned in the previous chapter you don't need the
               <span class="code">
                h:inputHidden
               </span>
               element, so just keep it away.
              </p>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#SaveEditedDataItem" name="SaveEditedDataItem">
                Save edited data item
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               Saving is simple, the JSF lifecycle already has updated the MyData item for you. Just do your DAO update thing.
              </p>
              <p>
               The relevant java code of the backing bean:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String saveDataItem() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Retain the ID of the data item from hidden input element.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               .setId(Long.valueOf(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItemId
               </span>
               .getValue().toString()));
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Do your "UPDATE mydata SET values WHERE id" thing.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                try
               </span>
               {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataDAO
               </span>
               .save(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               );
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                catch
               </span>
               (DAOException e) {
            setErrorMessage(e.getMessage() +
               <span class="codevalue">
                " Cause: "
               </span>
               + e.getCause());
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codevalue">
                "list"
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Navigation case.
               </span>
               }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               <b>
                Session scope:
               </b>
               the hidden input element is not needed, so you can safely remove the related code lines.
              </p>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#EditableDatatable" name="EditableDatatable">
                Editable datatable
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You can also use the datatable to mass-edit the datalist. Also here saving the edited datalist is simple, the JSF lifecycle already has updated the dataList for you. You just need to do your DAO update thing.
              </p>
              <p>
               The relevant JSF code looks like:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:inputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.name}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:inputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.value}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;br/&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Save"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.saveDataList}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               The relevant java code of the backing bean:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String saveDataList() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Do your "UPDATE mydata SET values WHERE id" thing for each data item.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                try
               </span>
               {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataDAO
               </span>
               .save(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               );
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                catch
               </span>
               (DAOException e) {
            setErrorMessage(e.getMessage() +
               <span class="codevalue">
                " Cause: "
               </span>
               + e.getCause());
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codevalue">
                "list"
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Navigation case.
               </span>
               }

}
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#AddNewRowsToDatatable" name="AddNewRowsToDatatable">
                Add new rows to datatable
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               Adding new rows to the datatable is in fact easy, just add a new and empty
               <span class="code">
                MyData
               </span>
               item to the
               <span class="code">
                dataList
               </span>
               and let the
               <span class="code">
                rendered
               </span>
               attribute of the components intercept on the ID being null. Also add a counter to inform the bean how many rows are been added so that it knows how to prepare the list and how many of the last rows have to be saved.
              </p>
              <p>
               But in the request scope you'll have to store the counter in a
               <span class="code">
                HtmlInputHidden
               </span>
               component bound to the page so that its value can be retained in the next request, regardless the outcome of the validations phase.
              </p>
              <p>
               The relevant JSF code looks like:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id}"
               </span>
               rendered=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id != null}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "new"
               </span>
               rendered=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id == null}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>

               </span>

               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">

               </span>
               <span class="codetag">

               </span>

               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.name}"
               </span>
               rendered=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id != null}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:inputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.name}"
               </span>
               rendered=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id == null}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.value}"
               </span>
               rendered=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id != null}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:inputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.value}"
               </span>
               rendered=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id == null}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;br/&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:inputHidden
               </span>
               binding=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.addCount}"
               </span>
               converter=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "javax.faces.Integer"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Add"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.addNewDataItem}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Save"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.saveNewDataItems}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               The relevant java code of the backing bean (note that you should preload the
               <span class="code">
                dataList
               </span>
               by lazy loading in the getter and that the
               <span class="code">
                loadDataList()
               </span>
               method is updated):
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlInputHidden;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               HtmlInputHidden
               <span class="codeproperty">
                addCount
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlInputHidden();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Constructors ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               MyBean() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Preset it to 0 to avoid NullPointerExceptions.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                addCount
               </span>
               .setValue(0);
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               loadDataList() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Do your "SELECT * FROM mydata" thing.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                try
               </span>
               {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataDAO
               </span>
               .list();
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                catch
               </span>
               (DAOException e) {
            setErrorMessage(e.getMessage() +
               <span class="codevalue">
                " Cause: "
               </span>
               + e.getCause());
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // If any, prepare the list with the new added items.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                for
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               i = 0; i addCount.getValue(); i++) {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               .add(
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               MyData());
        }
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String addNewDataItem() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Add new MyData item to the data list.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               .add(
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               MyData());
               <span class="codeproperty">
                addCount
               </span>
               .setValue(((Integer)
               <span class="codeproperty">
                addCount
               </span>
               .getValue()) + 1);
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Postback to same view. You can declare method void as well.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String saveNewDataItems() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Do your "UPDATE mydata SET values WHERE id" thing for each new data item.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                try
               </span>
               {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               size =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               .size();
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataDAO
               </span>
               .save(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               .subList(size - ((Integer)
               <span class="codeproperty">
                addCount
               </span>
               .getValue()), size));
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                catch
               </span>
               (DAOException e) {
            setErrorMessage(e.getMessage() +
               <span class="codevalue">
                " Cause: "
               </span>
               + e.getCause());
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Reset the amount of newly added items.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                addCount
               </span>
               .setValue(0);
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codevalue">
                "list"
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Navigation case.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt; getDataList() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ==
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) {
            loadDataList();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Preload by lazy loading.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               HtmlInputHidden getAddCount() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                addCount
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Setters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setAddCount(HtmlInputHidden addCount) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                addCount
               </span>
               = addCount;
    }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               <b>
                Session scope:
               </b>
               as you don't need to retain the amount of newly added items in the next request -because the complete list already been kept in the session-, you can just remove the
               <span class="code">
                addCount
               </span>
               property and its getter and setter. Finally replace the property by a simple
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               property:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
