               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                addCount
               </span>
               ;
              </pre>
              <p>
               Update the code in the action methods accordingly. Use it to increment the value in the
               <span class="code">
                addNewDataItem()
               </span>
               method, to get the sublist in the
               <span class="code">
                saveNewDataItems()
               </span>
               method and set its value to 0. No getter and setter is needed. Also the
               <span class="code">
                h:inputHidden
               </span>
               in the JSF page is not needed.
              </p>
              <p>
               If you're using the
               <span class="code">
                FacesContext.getCurrentInstance().getRenderResponse()
               </span>
               trick in the
               <span class="code">
                getDataList()
               </span>
               , then realize that it would override the newly added data items. So remove it or change the code accordingly that it will only reload the datalist in the action methods, e.g. after the save action.
              </p>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#SelectMultipleRows" name="SelectMultipleRows">
                Select multiple rows
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You also can select multiple rows using checkboxes. There are in general two ways to achieve this: one by adding a
               <span class="codekeyword">
                boolean
               </span>
               property to the DTO and another by adding a
               <span class="code">
                Map&lt;SomeIDType, Boolean&gt;
               </span>
               to the backing bean.
              </p>
              <p>
               Here is the first way: just add a
               <span class="codekeyword">
                boolean
               </span>
               property to the
               <b>
                MyData.java
               </b>
               DTO class and use
               <span class="code">
                h:selectBooleanCheckbox
               </span>
               to add a checkbox column which triggers this property.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyData {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                boolean
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selected
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                boolean
               </span>
               isSelected() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selected
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Setters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setSelected(
               <span class="codekeyword">
                boolean
               </span>
               selected) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selected
               </span>
               = selected;
    }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               Extend the datatable with a checkbox column and add a commandbutton to the form:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Select"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:selectBooleanCheckbox
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.selected}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Get selected items"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.getSelectedItems}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               Finally add the commandbutton action to the backing bean to get the selected items:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.ArrayList;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.Iterator;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.List;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt;
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedDataList
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String getSelectedItems() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Get selected items.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedDataList
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               ArrayList&lt;MyData&gt;();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                for
               </span>
               (MyData dataItem :
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (dataItem.isSelected()) {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedDataList
               </span>
               .add(dataItem);
                dataItem.setSelected(
               <span class="codekeyword">
                false
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Reset.
               </span>
               }
        }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Do your thing with the MyData items in List selectedDataList.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codevalue">
                "selected"
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Navigation case.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt; getSelectedDataList() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedDataList
               </span>
               ;
    }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               Here is the another way. If you do not want to extend the
               <span class="code">
                MyData
               </span>
               object with the
               <span class="codekeyword">
                boolean
               </span>
               property
               <span class="code">
                selected
               </span>
               for some reasons, then you can also consider the following approach with a
               <span class="code">
                Map&lt;SomeIDType, Boolean&gt;
               </span>
               where the
               <span class="code">
                SomeIDType
               </span>
               must represent the same type as the unique ID of the DAO, in this case
               <span class="code">
                Long
               </span>
               :
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Select"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:selectBooleanCheckbox
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.selectedIds[dataItem.id]}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Get selected items"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.getSelectedItems}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               The appropriate backing bean code:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.ArrayList;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.HashMap;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.Iterator;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.List;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.Map;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               Map&lt;Long, Boolean&gt;
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedIds
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HashMap&lt;Long, Boolean&gt;();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt;
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedDataList
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String getSelectedItems() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Get selected items.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedDataList
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               ArrayList&lt;MyData&gt;();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                for
               </span>
               (MyData dataItem :
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedIds
               </span>
               .get(dataItem.getId()).booleanValue()) {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedDataList
               </span>
               .add(dataItem);
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedIds
               </span>
               .remove(dataItem.getId());
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Reset.
               </span>
               }
        }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Do your thing with the MyData items in List selectedDataList.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codevalue">
                "selected"
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Navigation case.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               Map&lt;Long, Boolean&gt; getSelectedIds() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedIds
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt; getSelectedDataList() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                selectedDataList
               </span>
               ;
    }

}
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#SelectRowByRadioButton" name="SelectRowByRadioButton">
                Select row by radio button
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               Using
               <span class="code">
                h:selectOneRadio
               </span>
               in a JSF datatable is a bit tricky. When putting just a
               <span class="code">
                h:selectOneRadio
               </span>
               component in a
               <span class="code">
                h:column
               </span>
               column, the radio buttons gets rendered, but they are not grouped together. Each radio button is attached to one row object and not to the datatable itself, resulting the other radiobuttons not getting unselected when you select one radiobutton. To get it work, use JavaScript to unselect all other radio buttons when one radio button is selected. This is only good for the human eye.
              </p>
              <p>
               The real work is done by the
               <span class="code">
                valuechangelistener
               </span>
               attribute of the
               <span class="code">
                h:selectOneRadio
               </span>
               which fires a
               <span class="code">
                ValueChangeEvent
               </span>
               . When you clicks a radio button inside a row and then clicks the command button
               <b>
                outside
               </b>
               the row, the row index of the selected row will be lost. The fired
               <span class="code">
                ValueChangeEvent
               </span>
               is processed during the third phase of the
               <a href="/2006/09/debug-jsf-lifecycle.html">
                JSF lifecycle
               </a>
               , where the row index is still available. The row index is reset during the fourth phase and the command button action is invoked during the fifth phase. So the trick is to store the object of the selected row during the processing of the
               <span class="code">
                ValueChangeEvent
               </span>
               and finally handle with it during the command button action.
              </p>
              <p>
               Add a
               <span class="code">
                h:selectOneRadio
               </span>
               column to the datatable and supply a fake selectItem to it:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               binding=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataTable}"
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Select"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:selectOneRadio
               </span>
               valueChangeListener=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.setSelectedItem}"
               </span>
               onclick=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataTableSelectOneRadio(this);"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:selectItem
               </span>
               itemValue=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "null"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:selectOneRadio&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Get selected item"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.getSelectedItem}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               Add the valuechangelistener and the commandbutton action to the backing bean to get the selected item and to handle with it:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.event.ValueChangeEvent;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setSelectedItem(ValueChangeEvent event) {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Catch the MyData item during the third phase of the JSF lifecycle.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               = (MyData) dataTable.getRowData();
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String getSelectedItem() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // The MyData item is already catched in setSelectedItem().
               </span>
               selectedDataList =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               ArrayList&lt;MyData&gt;();
        selectedDataList.add(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Do your thing with the MyData item in List selectedDataList.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codevalue">
                "selected"
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Navigation case.
               </span>
               }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               Here is the JavaScript function which resets all other radio buttons of the same column.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                function
               </span>
               dataTableSelectOneRadio(radio) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                var
               </span>
               id = radio.name.substring(radio.name.lastIndexOf(
               <span class="codevalue">
                ':'
               </span>
               ));
               <span class="codekeyword">
                var
               </span>
               el = radio.form.elements;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                for
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codekeyword">
                var
               </span>
               i = 0; i if (el[i].name.substring(el[i].name.lastIndexOf(
               <span class="codevalue">
                ':'
               </span>
               )) == id) {
            el[i].checked =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                false
               </span>
               ;
        }
    }
    radio.checked =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                true
               </span>
               ;
}
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#SortingDatatable" name="SortingDatatable">
                Sorting datatable
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               <small>
                <b>
                 Update
                </b>
                : there's a newer article out for more effective sorting at DAO level. You may find it useful:
                <a href="http://balusc.blogspot.com/2008/10/effective-datatable-paging-and-sorting.html" target="_blank">
                 Effective datatable paging and sorting
                </a>
                .
               </small>
              </p>
              <p>
               As datatables can be filled with
               <span class="code">
                List
               </span>
               objects, you can easily sort a datatable using
               <span class="code">
                <a href="http://java.sun.com/j2se/1.5.0/docs/api/java/util/Collections.html#sort(java.util.List,%20java.util.Comparator)" target="_blank">
                 Collections.sort()
                </a>
               </span>
               . The best approach is to add a
               <span class="code">
                h:commandLink
               </span>
               tag with one
               <span class="code">
                <a href="/2006/06/communication-in-jsf.html">
                 f:attribute
                </a>
               </span>
               tag to each column header. The
               <span class="code">
                h:commandLink
               </span>
               tag should invoke the sorting in the backing bean. The
               <span class="code">
                f:attribute
               </span>
               tag should pass the column name/type, or in this case, the name of the field getter of the DTO class. And it should be nice to reverse the sorting when clicking again at the same column header.
              </p>
              <p>
               Add commandlinks with params to the column headers of the datatable:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               binding=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataTable}"
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandLink
               </span>
               actionListener=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.sortDataList}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:attribute
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "sortField"
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "getId"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:commandLink&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandLink
               </span>
               actionListener=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.sortDataList}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:attribute
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "sortField"
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "getName"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:commandLink&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.name}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandLink
               </span>
               actionListener=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.sortDataList}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:attribute
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "sortField"
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "getValue"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:commandLink&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.value}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:inputHidden
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.sortField}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:inputHidden
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.sortAscending}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               <b>
                Session scope:
               </b>
               you don't need the
               <span class="code">
                h:inputHidden
               </span>
               elements as the current
               <span class="code">
                sortField
               </span>
               and
               <span class="code">
                sortAscending
               </span>
               won't be garbaged after one request.
              </p>
              <p>
               Now extend the backing bean with
               <span class="code">
                sortDataList()
               </span>
               to set the sort field and the sort order. Use the
               <span class="code">
                f:attribute value
               </span>
               to indicate which MyData field should be sorted. The
               <span class="code">
                DTOComparator
               </span>
               is described later.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.Collections;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.context.FacesContext;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               myutil.DTOComparator;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               String
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortField
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                boolean
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortAscending
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                true
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               sortDataList(ActionEvent event) {
        String sortFieldAttribute = getAttribute(event,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "sortField"
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Get and set sort field and sort order.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortField
               </span>
               !=
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               &amp;&amp;
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortField
               </span>
               .equals(sortFieldAttribute)) {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortAscending
               </span>
               = !
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortAscending
               </span>
               ;
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                else
               </span>
               {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortField
               </span>
               = sortFieldAttribute;
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortAscending
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                true
               </span>
               ;
        }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Sort results.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortField
               </span>
               !=
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) {
            Collections.sort(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               DTOComparator(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortField
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortAscending
               </span>
               ));
        }
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String getSortField() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortField
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                boolean
               </span>
               getSortAscending() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortAscending
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Setters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setSortField(String sortField) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortField
               </span>
               = sortField;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setSortAscending(boolean sortAscending) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortAscending
               </span>
               = sortAscending;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Helpers -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                static
               </span>
               String getAttribute(ActionEvent event, String name) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               (String) event.getComponent().getAttributes().get(name);
    }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               <b>
                Session scope:
               </b>
               you don't need to pre-instantiate the
               <span class="code">
                sortField
               </span>
               and
               <span class="code">
                sortAscending
               </span>
               with
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               and
               <span class="codekeyword">
                true
               </span>
               as those won't be garbaged after one request. You also have to move the piece of Java code after the "
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Sort results.
               </span>
               " comment at the end of
               <span class="code">
                sortDataList
               </span>
               to the end of
               <span class="code">
                loadDataList
               </span>
               . This is because the reloading of the
               <span class="code">
                dataList
               </span>
               in the
               <span class="code">
                getDataList()
               </span>
               method will override the sorting otherwise.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               loadDataList() {

        ...
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Sort results.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (sortField !=
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) {
            Collections.sort(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               DTOComparator(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortField
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codeproperty">
                sortAscending
               </span>
               ));
        }
    }
              </pre>
              <p>
               Here is the
               <b>
                DTOComparator.java
               </b>
               which can be very useful to sort data transfer objects in a
               <span class="code">
                List
               </span>
               . It implements the
               <span class="code">
                <a href="http://java.sun.com/j2se/1.5.0/docs/api/java/util/Comparator.html" target="_blank">
                 Comparator
                </a>
               </span>
               interface.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               myutil;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.ArrayList;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.Comparator;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.Iterator;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.List;
               <span class="codecomment2">
                /**
 * Sorts a collection of data transfer objects (DTO's) based on the name of the getter of the field
 * to sort on. For example: the DTO MyData has three fields ID, Name and Value, all with appropriate
 * getters and setters. If you want to sort on the field Name, which has a getter called "getName",
 * then invoke the sorting as follows:
 * &lt;pre&gt;
 * Collections.sort(dataList, new DTOComparator("getName", true));
 * &lt;/pre&gt;
 * The following call is also supported. The "get" will be prefixed automatically if not present:
 * &lt;pre&gt;
 * Collections.sort(dataList, new DTOComparator("name", true));
 * &lt;/pre&gt;
 * You can use "deep" getters when a DTO contains one or more nested DTO's. For example: MyData1
 * contains a MyData2 property which contains a String property "name". If you want to sort
 * myData1List on the "name" property of MyData2, then separate the getters by dots and invoke the
 * sorting as follows:
 * &lt;pre&gt;
 * Collections.sort(myData1List, new DTOComparator("myData2.name", true));
 * &lt;/pre&gt;
 * The boolean 2nd parameter indicates the sort order. If true, then the collection will be sorted
 * ascending at natural sort order. If false, then the collection will be sorted descending at
 * natural sort order. The default value is true.
 * &lt;p&gt;
 * Very useful for lists of DTO's used in JSF datatables.
 *
 *
                <b>
                 @author
                </b>
                BalusC
 *
                <b>
                 @link
                </b>
                http://balusc.blogspot.com/2006/06/using-datatables.html
 */
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               DTOComparator
               <span class="codekeyword">
                implements
               </span>
               Comparator&lt;Object&gt; {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               List&lt;String&gt;
               <span class="codeproperty">
                getters
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                boolean
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                ascending
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Constructor -------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment2">
                /**
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment2">
                *
                <b>
                 @param
                </b>
                getter The name of the getter of the field to sort on.
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment2">
                *
                <b>
                 @param
                </b>
                ascending The sort order: true = ascending, false = descending.
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment2">
                */
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               DTOComparator(String getter,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                boolean
               </span>
               ascending) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                getters
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               ArrayList&lt;String&gt;();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                for
               </span>
               (String name : getter.split(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "\\."
               </span>
               )) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (!name.startsWith(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "get"
               </span>
               )) {
                name =
               <span class="codevalue">
                "get"
               </span>
               + name.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase() + name.substring(1);
            }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                getters
               </span>
               .add(name);
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                ascending
               </span>
               = ascending;
    }
               <span class="codecomment2">
                /**
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment2">
                *
                <b>
                 @param
                </b>
                getter The name of the getter of the field to sort on.
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment2">
                */
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               DTOComparator(String getter) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               (getter,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                true
               </span>
               );
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment2">
                /**
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment2">
                *
                <b>
                 @see
                </b>
                java.util.Comparator#compare(java.lang.Object, java.lang.Object)
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment2">
                */
               </span>
               <span class="codeannotation">
                @SuppressWarnings
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codevalue">
                "unchecked"
               </span>
               )
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               compare(Object o1, Object o2) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                try
               </span>
               {
            Iterator&lt;String&gt; iter =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                getters
               </span>
               .iterator();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                while
               </span>
               (o1 !=
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               &amp;&amp; o2 !=
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               &amp;&amp; iter.hasNext()) {
                String getter = iter.next();
                o1 = o1.getClass().getMethod(getter,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               Class[0]).invoke(o1,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               Object[0]);
                o2 = o2.getClass().getMethod(getter,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               Class[0]).invoke(o2,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               Object[0]);
            }
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                catch
               </span>
               (Exception e) {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // If this exception occurs, then it is usually a fault of the DTO developer.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                throw
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               RuntimeException(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Cannot compare "
               </span>
               + o1 +
               <span class="codevalue">
                " with "
               </span>
               + o2 +
               <span class="codevalue">
                " on "
               </span>
               +
               <span class="codeproperty">
                getters
               </span>
               , e);
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codeproperty">
                ascending
               </span>
               ) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               (o1 ==
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) ? -1 : ((o2 ==
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) ? 1 : ((Comparable&lt;Object&gt;) o1).compareTo(o2));
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                else
               </span>
               {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               (o2 ==
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) ? -1 : ((o1 ==
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) ? 1 : ((Comparable&lt;Object&gt;) o2).compareTo(o1));
        }
    }

}
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#PagingDatatable" name="PagingDatatable">
                Paging datatable
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               <small>
                <b>
                 Update
                </b>
                : there's a newer article out for a more effective paging at DAO level. You may find it useful:
                <a href="http://balusc.blogspot.com/2008/10/effective-datatable-paging-and-sorting.html" target="_blank">
                 Effective datatable paging and sorting
                </a>
                .
               </small>
              </p>
              <p>
               If you have a plenty of rows, then you can use the following datatable attributes to page through the datatable:
               <span class="code">
                first
               </span>
               and
               <span class="code">
                rows
               </span>
               . The
               <span class="code">
                first
               </span>
               attribute identifies the row number of the starting row which should be displayed. The
               <span class="code">
                rows
               </span>
               attribute identifies the amount of rows to be shown at once, from the first row on. For pagination we need to set the
               <span class="code">
                first
               </span>
               attribute dynamically in the backing bean. You can use commandlinks or commandbuttons to change this value.
              </p>
              <p>
               So extend the datatable with the
               <span class="code">
                rows
               </span>
               attribute and a set of commandbuttons in the footer. In this example we will page on every 3 rows.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               binding=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataTable}"
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               rows=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "3"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "footer"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:panelGroup&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "first"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.pageFirst}"
               </span>
               disabled=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataTable.first == 0}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "prev"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.pagePrevious}"
               </span>
               disabled=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataTable.first == 0}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "next"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.pageNext}"
               </span>
               disabled=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataTable.first + myBean.dataTable.rows
                        &gt;= myBean.dataTable.rowCount}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "last"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.pageLast}"
               </span>
               disabled=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataTable.first + myBean.dataTable.rows
                        &gt;= myBean.dataTable.rowCount}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:panelGroup&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               Please note the
               <span class="code">
                disabled
               </span>
               attribute of the commandbuttons. The 'first' and the 'prev' buttons should be disabled at the first page. The 'next' and the 'last' buttons should be disabled when a next page cannot exist.
              </p>
              <p>
               And add the following pagination methods to the backing bean:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               pageFirst() {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .setFirst(0);
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               pagePrevious() {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .setFirst(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .getFirst() -
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .getRows());
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               pageNext() {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .setFirst(
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .getFirst() +
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .getRows());
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               pageLast() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               count =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .getRowCount();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               rows =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .getRows();
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .setFirst(count - ((count % rows != 0) ? count % rows : rows));
    }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               With the following getters you can get the current page number and the total number of pages.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Special getters ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               getCurrentPage() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               rows =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .getRows();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               first =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .getFirst();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               count =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .getRowCount();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               (count / rows) - ((count - first) / rows) + 1;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               getTotalPages() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               rows =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .getRows();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               count =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTable
               </span>
               .getRowCount();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               (count / rows) + ((count % rows != 0) ? 1 : 0);
    }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               Note that you need to handle
               <span class="code">
                ArithmeticException / by zero
               </span>
               when the
               <span class="code">
                rows
               </span>
               is 0 and you still want to display the table.
              </p>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#NestingDatatables" name="NestingDatatables">
                Nesting datatables
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You can use multidimensional lists in a nested datatable: just put the inner datatable in a
               <span class="code">
                h:column
               </span>
               of the outer datatable and add the inner list to the DTO of the outer list.
              </p>
              <p>
               The basic JSF code:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.name}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.value}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.innerList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "innerItem"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{innerItem.name}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{innerItem.value}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               The updated Java code of
               <b>
                MyData.java
               </b>
               which represents each
               <span class="code">
                dataItem
               </span>
               :
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyData {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt;
               <span class="codeproperty">
                innerList
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt; getInnerList() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                innerList
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Setters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setInnerList(List&lt;MyData&gt; innerList) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                innerList
               </span>
               = innerList;
    }

}
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#PopulateDatatable" name="PopulateDatatable">
                Populate datatable
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You can also programmatically populate the datatable in the backing bean. This may be useful if you don't know the expected state of the datatable in the JSF page, but only in the backing bean.
              </p>
              <p>
               Here is the basic JSF code:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:panelGroup
               </span>
               binding=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataTableGroup}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               Fairly simple, isn't it? We're using a
               <span class="code">
                h:panelGroup
               </span>
               as placeholder, because when you want to bind the datatable itself, then you
               <i>
                have
               </i>
               to specify the
               <span class="code">
                var
               </span>
               attribute in the JSF page. Using a
               <span class="code">
                h:panelGroup
               </span>
               without any style doesn't output anything to the HTML, so this won't harm that much. This approach is not needed anymore if you're using JSF 1.2_10 or newer, since this
