               <a href="https://javaserverfaces.dev.java.net/issues/show_bug.cgi?id=774" target="_blank">
                bug
               </a>
               is been fixed.
              </p>
              <p>
               And here is the relevant Java code of the backing bean, it might look like a lot of code, but it is actually rather simple:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.List;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.el.ValueExpression;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlColumn;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlDataTable;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlOutputText;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlPanelGroup;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               HtmlPanelGroup
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTableGroup
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Placeholder.
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               populateDataTable() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:dataTable value="#{myBean.dataList}" var="dataItem"&gt;.
               </span>
               HtmlDataTable dataTable =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlDataTable();
        dataTable.setValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "value"
               </span>
               ,
            createValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               , List.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
        dataTable.setVar(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:column&gt; for 'ID' column.
               </span>
               HtmlColumn idColumn =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlColumn();
        dataTable.getChildren().add(idColumn);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="ID"&gt; for &lt;f:facet name="header"&gt; of 'ID' column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText idHeader =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
        idHeader.setValue(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID"
               </span>
               );
        idColumn.setHeader(idHeader);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="#{dataItem.id}"&gt; for the body of 'ID' column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText idOutput =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
        idOutput.setValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "value"
               </span>
               ,
            createValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id}"
               </span>
               , Long.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
        idColumn.getChildren().add(idOutput);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:column&gt; for 'Name' column.
               </span>
               HtmlColumn nameColumn =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlColumn();
        dataTable.getChildren().add(nameColumn);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="Name"&gt; for &lt;f:facet name="header"&gt; of 'Name' column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText nameHeader =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
        nameHeader.setValue(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name"
               </span>
               );
        nameColumn.setHeader(nameHeader);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="#{dataItem.name}"&gt; for the body of 'Name' column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText nameOutput =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
        nameOutput.setValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "value"
               </span>
               ,
            createValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.name}"
               </span>
               , String.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
        nameColumn.getChildren().add(nameOutput);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:column&gt; for 'Value' column.
               </span>
               HtmlColumn valueColumn =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlColumn();
        dataTable.getChildren().add(valueColumn);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="Value"&gt; for &lt;f:facet name="header"&gt; of 'Value' column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText valueHeader =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
        valueHeader.setValue(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value"
               </span>
               );
        valueColumn.setHeader(valueHeader);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="#{dataItem.value}"&gt; for the body of 'Value' column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText valueOutput =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
        valueOutput.setValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "value"
               </span>
               ,
            createValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.value}"
               </span>
               , String.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
        valueColumn.getChildren().add(valueOutput);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Finally add the datatable to &lt;h:panelGroup binding="#{myBean.dataTableGroup}"&gt;.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTableGroup
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlPanelGroup();
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTableGroup
               </span>
               .getChildren().add(dataTable);
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               HtmlPanelGroup getDataTableGroup() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // This will be called once in the first RESTORE VIEW phase.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTableGroup
               </span>
               ==
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) {
            populateDataTable();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Populate datatable.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTableGroup
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Setters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>

               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataTableGroup
               </span>
               = dataTableGroup;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Helpers -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               ValueExpression createValueExpression(String valueExpression, Class&lt;?&gt; valueType) {
        FacesContext facesContext = FacesContext.getCurrentInstance();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               facesContext.getApplication().getExpressionFactory().createValueExpression(
            facesContext.getELContext(), valueExpression, valueType);
    }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               This creates exactly the same datatable as shown in
               <a href="#ShowDataContentsInDatatable">

               </a>

              </p>

              <h4>
               <a href="#PopulateActionDatatable" name="PopulateActionDatatable">
                Populate action datatable
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You can also programmatically populate a datatable with a binding and a backing bean action in every row in the backing bean. This may be useful if you don't know the expected state of the datatable in the JSF page, but only in the backing bean.
              </p>
              <p>
               Here is the basic JSF code:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:panelGroup
               </span>
               binding=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.actionDataTableGroup}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               Fairly simple, isn't it? We're using a
               <span class="code">
                h:panelGroup
               </span>
               as placeholder, because when you want to bind the datatable itself, then you
               <i>
                have
               </i>
               to specify the
               <span class="code">
                var
               </span>
               attribute in the JSF page. Using a
               <span class="code">
                h:panelGroup
               </span>
               without any style doesn't output anything to the HTML, so this won't harm that much. This approach is not needed anymore if you're using JSF 1.2_10 or newer, since this
               <a href="https://javaserverfaces.dev.java.net/issues/show_bug.cgi?id=774" target="_blank">
                bug
               </a>
               is been fixed.
              </p>
              <p>
               And here is the relevant Java code of the backing bean, it might look like a lot of code, but it is actually rather simple:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.List;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.el.MethodExpression;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.el.ValueExpression;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlColumn;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlCommandLink;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlDataTable;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlInputText;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlOutputText;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlPanelGroup;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>

                private
               </span>
               HtmlPanelGroup
               <span class="codeproperty">
                actionDataTableGroup
               </span>

                // Placeholder.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               HtmlDataTable
               <span class="codeproperty">
                actionDataTable
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               populateActionDataTable() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:dataTable binding="#{myBean.dataTable}"
        // value="#{myBean.dataList}" var="dataItem"&gt;.
               </span>
               HtmlDataTable actionDataTable =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlDataTable();
        actionDataTable.setValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "binding"
               </span>
               ,
            createValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.actionDataTable}"
               </span>
               , HtmlDataTable.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
        actionDataTable.setValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "value"
               </span>
               ,
            createValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               , List.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
        actionDataTable.setVar(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:column&gt; for 'ID' column.
               </span>
               HtmlColumn idColumn =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlColumn();
        actionDataTable.getChildren().add(idColumn);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="ID"&gt; for &lt;f:facet name="header"&gt; of 'ID' column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText idHeader =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
        idHeader.setValue(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID"
               </span>
               );
        idColumn.setHeader(idHeader);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:commandLink value="#{dataItem.id}" action="#{myBean.editPopulatedDataItem}" /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // for the body of 'ID' column.
               </span>
               HtmlCommandLink idLink =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlCommandLink();
        idLink.setId(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "edit"
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Custom ID is required in dynamic UIInput and UICommand.
               </span>
               idLink.setValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "value"
               </span>
               ,
            createValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id}"
               </span>
               , Long.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
        idLink.setActionExpression(
            createActionExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.editPopulatedDataItem}"
               </span>
               , String.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
        idColumn.getChildren().add(idLink);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:column&gt; for 'Name' column.
               </span>
               HtmlColumn nameColumn =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlColumn();
        actionDataTable.getChildren().add(nameColumn);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="Name"&gt; for &lt;f:facet name="header"&gt; of 'Name' column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText nameHeader =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
        nameHeader.setValue(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name"
               </span>
               );
        nameColumn.setHeader(nameHeader);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="#{dataItem.name}"&gt; for the body of 'Name' column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText nameOutput =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
        nameOutput.setValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "value"
               </span>
               ,
            createValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.name}"
               </span>
               , String.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
        nameColumn.getChildren().add(nameOutput);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:column&gt; for 'Value' column.
               </span>
               HtmlColumn valueColumn =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlColumn();
        actionDataTable.getChildren().add(valueColumn);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="Value"&gt; for &lt;f:facet name="header"&gt; of 'Value' column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText valueHeader =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
        valueHeader.setValue(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value"
               </span>
               );
        valueColumn.setHeader(valueHeader);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="#{dataItem.value}"&gt; for the body of 'Value' column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText valueOutput =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
        valueOutput.setValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "value"
               </span>
               ,
            createValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.value}"
               </span>
               , String.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
        valueColumn.getChildren().add(valueOutput);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Finally add the datatable to &lt;h:panelGroup binding="#{myBean.actionDataTableGroup}"&gt;.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                actionDataTableGroup
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlPanelGroup();
               <span class="codeproperty">
                actionDataTableGroup
               </span>
               .getChildren().add(actionDataTable);
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String editPopulatedDataItem() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Get selected MyData item to be edited.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               = (MyData)
               <span class="codeproperty">
                actionDataTable
               </span>
               .getRowData();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codevalue">
                "edit"
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Navigation case.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               HtmlPanelGroup getActionDataTableGroup() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // This will be called once in the first RESTORE VIEW phase.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codeproperty">
                actionDataTableGroup
               </span>
               ==
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) {
            populateActionDataTable();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Populate action datatable.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                actionDataTableGroup
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               HtmlDataTable getActionDataTable() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                actionDataTable
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Setters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">

               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                actionDataTableGroup
               </span>
               = actionDataTableGroup;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setActionDataTable(HtmlDataTable actionDataTable) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                actionDataTable
               </span>
               = actionDataTable;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Helpers -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               ValueExpression createValueExpression(String valueExpression, Class&lt;?&gt; valueType) {
        FacesContext facesContext = FacesContext.getCurrentInstance();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               facesContext.getApplication().getExpressionFactory().createValueExpression(
            facesContext.getELContext(), valueExpression, valueType);
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               MethodExpression createActionExpression(String actionExpression, Class&lt;?&gt; returnType) {
        FacesContext facesContext = FacesContext.getCurrentInstance();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               facesContext.getApplication().getExpressionFactory().createMethodExpression(
            facesContext.getELContext(), actionExpression, returnType,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               Class[0]);
    }

              <p>
               This creates exactly the same datatable as shown in

              <h4>
               <a href="#PopulateEditableDatatable" name="PopulateEditableDatatable">
                Populate editable datatable
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You can also programmatically populate an editable datatable in the backing bean. This may be useful if you don't know the expected state of the datatable in the JSF page, but only in the backing bean.
              </p>
              <p>
               Here is the basic JSF code:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:panelGroup
               </span>
               binding=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.editableDataTableGroup}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               Fairly simple, isn't it? We're using a
               <span class="code">
                h:panelGroup
               </span>
               as placeholder, because when you want to bind the datatable itself, then you
               <i>
                have
               </i>
               to specify the
               <span class="code">
                var
               </span>
               attribute in the JSF page. Using a
               <span class="code">
                h:panelGroup
               </span>
               without any style doesn't output anything to the HTML, so this won't harm that much. This approach is not needed anymore if you're using JSF 1.2_10 or newer, since this
               <a href="https://javaserverfaces.dev.java.net/issues/show_bug.cgi?id=774" target="_blank">
                bug
               </a>
               is been fixed.
              </p>
              <p>
               And here is the relevant Java code of the backing bean, it might look like a lot of code, but it is actually rather simple:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.List;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.el.MethodExpression;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.el.ValueExpression;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlColumn;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlCommandButton;
               <span class="codekeyword">

               </span>

               </span>

                if

                editableDataTableGroup
               </span>
               ==
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) {
            populateEditableDataTable();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Populate editable datatable.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                editableDataTableGroup
               </span>
               ;
    }

               </span>
               = editableDataTableGroup;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Helpers -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               ValueExpression createValueExpression(String valueExpression, Class&lt;?&gt; valueType) {
        FacesContext facesContext = FacesContext.getCurrentInstance();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               facesContext.getApplication().getExpressionFactory().createValueExpression(
            facesContext.getELContext(), valueExpression, valueType);
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               MethodExpression createActionExpression(String actionExpression, Class&lt;?&gt; returnType) {
        FacesContext facesContext = FacesContext.getCurrentInstance();
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               facesContext.getApplication().getExpressionFactory().createMethodExpression(
            facesContext.getELContext(), actionExpression, returnType,
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               Class[0]);
    }

}
              </pre>
              <p>
               This creates exactly the same datatable as shown in
               <a href="#EditableDatatable">
                Editable datatable
               </a>
               .
              </p>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">

               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#PopulateDynamicDatatable" name="PopulateDynamicDatatable">
                Populate dynamic datatable
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You also can dynamically populate a datatable in the backing bean. This may be very useful if you are using dynamic generated two-dimensional lists (for example, uploaded CSV files, local text files, DB fields, etc) and you don't know the amount of columns before.
              </p>
              <p>
               The basic JSF code:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:panelGroup
               </span>
               binding=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dynamicDataTableGroup}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               The relevant Java code of the backing bean:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.ArrayList;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.Arrays;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.List;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.el.ValueExpression;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.HtmlColumn;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.HtmlOutputText;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.component.html.HtmlDataTable;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.context.FacesContext;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                static
               </span>
               List&lt;List&lt;String&gt;&gt;
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicList
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Simulate fake DB.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                static
               </span>
               String[]
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicHeaders
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Optional.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               HtmlPanelGroup
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicDataTableGroup
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Placeholder.
               </span>
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               loadDynamicList() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Set headers (optional).
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicHeaders
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               String[] {
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value"
               </span>
               };
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Set rows. This is a stub example, just do your dynamic thing.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicList
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               ArrayList&lt;List&lt;String&gt;&gt;();
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicList
               </span>
               .add(Arrays.asList(
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               String[] {
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID1"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name1"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value1"
               </span>
               }));
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicList
               </span>
               .add(Arrays.asList(
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               String[] {
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID2"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name2"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value2"
               </span>
               }));
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicList
               </span>
               .add(Arrays.asList(
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               String[] {
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID3"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name3"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value3"
               </span>
               }));
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicList
               </span>
               .add(Arrays.asList(
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               String[] {
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID4"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name4"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value4"
               </span>
               }));
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicList
               </span>
               .add(Arrays.asList(
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               String[] {
               <span class="codevalue">
                "ID5"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Name5"
               </span>
               ,
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Value5"
               </span>
               }));
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               populateDynamicDataTable() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:dataTable value="#{myBean.dynamicList}" var="dynamicItem"&gt;.
               </span>
               HtmlDataTable dynamicDataTable =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlDataTable();
        dynamicDataTable.setValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "value"
               </span>
               ,
            createValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dynamicList}"
               </span>
               , List.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
        dynamicDataTable.setVar(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dynamicItem"
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Iterate over columns.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                for
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codekeyword">
                int
               </span>
               i = 0; i // Create &lt;h:column&gt;.
            HtmlColumn column =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlColumn();
            dynamicDataTable.getChildren().add(column);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="dynamicHeaders[i]"&gt; for &lt;f:facet name="header"&gt; of column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText header =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
            header.setValue(dynamicHeaders[i]);
            column.setHeader(header);
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Create &lt;h:outputText value="#{dynamicItem[" + i + "]}"&gt; for the body of column.
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText output =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlOutputText();
            output.setValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "value"
               </span>
               ,
                createValueExpression(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dynamicItem["
               </span>
               + i +
               <span class="codevalue">
                "]}"
               </span>
               , String.
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               ));
            column.getChildren().add(output);
        }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Add the datatable to &lt;h:panelGroup binding="#{myBean.dynamicDataTableGroup}"&gt;.
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicDataTableGroup
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               HtmlPanelGroup();
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicDataTableGroup
               </span>
               .getChildren().add(dynamicDataTable);
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Getters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               HtmlPanelGroup getDynamicDataTableGroup() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // This will be called once in the first RESTORE VIEW phase.
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicDataTableGroup
               </span>
               ==
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               ) {
            loadDynamicList();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Preload dynamic list.
               </span>
               populateDynamicDataTable();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Populate editable datatable.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicDataTableGroup
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               List&lt;List&lt;String&gt;&gt; getDynamicList() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicList
               </span>
               ;
    }
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Setters -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                void
               </span>
               setDynamicDataTableGroup(HtmlPanelGroup dynamicDataTableGroup) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                this
               </span>
               .
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dynamicDataTableGroup
               </span>
               = dynamicDataTableGroup;
    }

}
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#AddRowNumbers" name="AddRowNumbers">
                Add row numbers
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               This is fairly simple to implement using
               <span class="code">
                getRowIndex()
               </span>
               method of the
               <span class="code">
                <a href="http://java.sun.com/javaee/javaserverfaces/1.2/docs/api/javax/faces/component/html/HtmlDataTable.html" target="_blank">
                 HtmlDataTable
                </a>
               </span>
               class, which is bound by
               <span class="code">
                h:dataTable binding.
               </span>
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               binding=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataTable}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:column&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:facet
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "header"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Row #"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:facet&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataTable.rowIndex + 1}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:column&gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               We are using + 1 in the value binding expression, because the row index usually starts with 0.
              </p>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#AlternatingRows" name="AlternatingRows">
                Alternating rows
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You can alternate the rows using the dataTable attribute
               <span class="code">
                rowClasses
               </span>
               and some piece of CSS. Put in there at least two style class names and the rows will apply those styles concurrently and repeating. Here is a basic example:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               rowClasses=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "row1, row2"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               Here is the CSS defining the
               <span class="code">
                row1
               </span>
               and
               <span class="code">
                row2
               </span>
               styles. This is just a basic example, you can define your own colors for example.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                .row1
               </span>
               {
    background-color:
               <span class="codevalue">
                #ddd
               </span>
               ;
}
               <span class="codekeyword">
                .row2
               </span>
               {
    background-color:
               <span class="codevalue">
                #bbb
               </span>
               ;
}
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#HighlightRowsOnClick" name="HighlightRowsOnClick">
                Highlight rows on click
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You can use Javascript and DOM to alter the rows of the dataTable by adding an onclick function to it which triggers a Javascript function. Here is a basic Javascript example:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                function
               </span>
               addOnclickToDatatableRows() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                var
               </span>
               trs = document.getElementById(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'dataTable'
               </span>
               ).getElementsByTagName(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'tbody'
               </span>
               )[0]
        .getElementsByTagName(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'tr'
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codekeyword">
                for
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codekeyword">
                var
               </span>
               i = 0; i new Function(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "highlightRow(this)"
               </span>
               );
    }
}
               <span class="codekeyword">
                function
               </span>
               highlightRow(tr) {
    tr.bgColor = (tr.bgColor !=
               <span class="codevalue">
                '#ff0000'
               </span>
               ) ?
               <span class="codevalue">
                '#ff0000'
               </span>
               :
               <span class="codevalue">
                '#ffffff'
               </span>
               ;
}
              </pre>
              <p>
               Call
               <span class="code">
                addOnclickToDatatableRows()
               </span>
               during onload of the window. Take note that the element ID in the Javascript have to be exactly the same as the rendered element ID of the table.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;head&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;script&gt;
               </span>
               window.onload = addOnclickToDatatableRows;
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/script&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/head&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;body&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               id=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataTable"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/body&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#HighlightAndSelectRowOnClick" name="HighlightAndSelectRowOnClick">
                Highlight and select row on click
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You can also highlight single row and select the row for submit using an onclick function on the table row. Basically just pass its row index to a plain vanilla HTML hidden input. Here is a basic Javascript example:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                function
               </span>
               addOnclickToDatatableRows() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                var
               </span>
               trs = document.getElementById(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'form:dataTable'
               </span>
               ).getElementsByTagName(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'tbody'
               </span>
               )[0]
        .getElementsByTagName(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'tr'
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codekeyword">
                for
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codekeyword">
                var
               </span>
               i = 0; i new Function(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "highlightAndSelectRow(this)"
               </span>
               );
    }
}
               <span class="codekeyword">
                function
               </span>
               highlightAndSelectRow(tr) {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                var
               </span>
               trs = document.getElementById(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'form:dataTable'
               </span>
               ).getElementsByTagName(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'tbody'
               </span>
               )[0]
        .getElementsByTagName(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'tr'
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codekeyword">
                for
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codekeyword">
                var
               </span>
               i = 0; i if (trs[i] == tr) {
            trs[i].bgColor =
               <span class="codevalue">
                '#ff0000'
               </span>
               ;
            document.form.rowIndex.value = trs[i].rowIndex;
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                else
               </span>
               {
            trs[i].bgColor =
               <span class="codevalue">
                '#ffffff'
               </span>
               ;
        }
    }
}
              </pre>
              <p>
               Call
               <span class="code">
                addOnclickToDatatableRows()
               </span>
               during onload of the window. Take note that the element ID in the Javascript have to be exactly the same as the generated element ID of the form and the table.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;head&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;script&gt;
               </span>
               window.onload = addOnclickToDatatableRows;
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/script&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/head&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;body&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form
               </span>
               id=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "form"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               id=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataTable"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;input
               </span>
               type=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "hidden"
               </span>
               name=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "rowIndex"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandButton
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "Edit selected row"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.editDataItem}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/body&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               Here is the relevant part of the backing bean code. This achieves exactly the same actions as shown in
               <a href="#AddBackingBeanActionToEveryRow">
                Add backing bean action to every row
               </a>
               and
               <a href="#GetSelectedDatatableRow">
                Get selected datatable row
               </a>
               :
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                package
               </span>
               mypackage;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               java.util.List;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                import
               </span>
               javax.faces.context.FacesContext;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                class
               </span>
               MyBean {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Init --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               List&lt;MyData&gt;
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codekeyword">
                private
               </span>
               MyData
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               MyData();
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Actions -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
               </span>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                public
               </span>
               String editDataItem() {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Obtain the row index from the hidden input element.
               </span>
               String rowIndex = FacesContext.getCurrentInstance().getExternalContext()
            .getRequestParameterMap().get(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "rowIndex"
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codekeyword">
                if
               </span>
               (rowIndex !=
               <span class="codekeyword">
                null
               </span>
               &amp;&amp; rowIndex.trim().length() != 0) {
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataItem
               </span>
               =
               <span class="codeproperty">
                dataList
               </span>
               .get(Integer.parseInt(rowIndex));
        }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                else
               </span>
               {
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Handle unexpected state, e.g. show message "Please select row" or so.
               </span>
               }
               <span class="codekeyword">
                return
               </span>
               <span class="codevalue">
                "edit"
               </span>
               ;
               <span class="codecomment1">
                // Navigation case.
               </span>
               }

}
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#HighlightRowsOnHover" name="HighlightRowsOnHover">
                Highlight rows on hover
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               You can use Javascript and DOM to alter the rows of the dataTable by adding an onmouseover and onmouseout function to it which triggers a Javascript function. Here is a basic Javascript example:
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codekeyword">
                function
               </span>
               addHoverToDatatableRows() {
               <span class="codekeyword">
                var
               </span>
               trs = document.getElementById(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'dataTable'
               </span>
               ).getElementsByTagName(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'tbody'
               </span>
               )[0]
        .getElementsByTagName(
               <span class="codevalue">
                'tr'
               </span>
               );
               <span class="codekeyword">
                for
               </span>
               (
               <span class="codekeyword">
                var
               </span>
               i = 0; i new Function(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "this.bgColor='#ff0000'"
               </span>
               );
        trs[i].onmouseout =
               <span class="codekeyword">
                new
               </span>
               Function(
               <span class="codevalue">
                "this.bgColor='#ffffff'"
               </span>
               );
    }
}
              </pre>
              <p>
               Call
               <span class="code">
                addHoverToDatatableRows()
               </span>
               during onload of the window. Take note that the element ID in the Javascript have to be exactly the same as the generated element ID of the table.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;head&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;script&gt;
               </span>
               window.onload = addHoverToDatatableRows;
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/script&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/head&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;body&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:dataTable
               </span>
               id=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataTable"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:dataTable&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/body&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#CustomizedTables" name="CustomizedTables">
                Customized tables
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               If you're using at least JSF 1.2 and
               <a href="https://maven-repository.dev.java.net/repository/jstl/jars/" target="_blank">
                JSTL 1.2
               </a>
               in a JSP 2.1 container (available in Java EE 5 server, e.g.
               <a href="http://tomcat.apache.org/download-60.cgi" target="_blank">
                Tomcat 6.0
               </a>
               or
               <a href="https://glassfish.dev.java.net//" target="_blank">
                Glassfish
               </a>
               ), then you can access JSF managed beans in the JSTL
               <span class="code">
                c:forEach
               </span>
               tag, thanks to the
               <a href="http://java.sun.com/products/jsp/reference/techart/unifiedEL.html" target="_blank">
                unified EL
               </a>
               . This will give you more freedom to create exotic tables based on a collection of DTO's from a managed bean, e.g. introducing colspans and so on.
              </p>
              <pre>
               <span class="codetagscript">
                &lt;%@
               </span>
               taglib uri=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "http://java.sun.com/jsp/jstl/core"
               </span>
               prefix=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "c"
               </span>
               <span class="codetagscript">
                %&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetagscript">
                &lt;%@
               </span>
               taglib uri=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "http://java.sun.com/jsf/core"
               </span>
               prefix=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "f"
               </span>
               <span class="codetagscript">
                %&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetagscript">
                &lt;%@
               </span>
               taglib uri=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "http://java.sun.com/jsf/html"
               </span>
               prefix=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "h"
               </span>
               <span class="codetagscript">
                %&gt;
               </span>
               ...
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:form&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;table&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;thead&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;tr&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;th
               </span>
               colspan=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "3"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               MASTER TABLE
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/th&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/tr&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;tr&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;th&gt;
               </span>
               ID
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/th&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;th&gt;
               </span>
               Name
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/th&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;th&gt;
               </span>
               Value
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/th&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/tr&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/thead&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;tbody&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;c:forEach
               </span>
               items=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataList}"
               </span>
               var=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "dataItem"
               </span>
               varStatus=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "status"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:verbatim
               </span>
               rendered=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id % 2 != 0}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;tr
               </span>
               style=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "background-color: red;"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;td
               </span>
               colspan=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "3"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               This is just an example of an alternately inserted row.
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/td&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/tr&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/f:verbatim&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;tr
               </span>
               style=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "background-color: ${status.index % 2 == 0 ? 'lightgray' : 'gray'};"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;td&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:commandLink
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.id}"
               </span>
               action=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.editDataItem}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;f:setPropertyActionListener
               </span>
               target=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{myBean.dataItem}"
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:commandLink&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/td&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;td&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.name}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/td&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;td&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;h:outputText
               </span>
               value=
               <span class="codevalue">
                "#{dataItem.value}"
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                /&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/td&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/tr&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/c:forEach&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/tbody&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/table&gt;
               </span>
               <span class="codetag">
                &lt;/h:form&gt;
               </span>
              </pre>
              <p>
               This creates a table with exactly the same behaviour as the table as shown in
               <a href="#AddBackingBeanActionToEveryRow">
                Add backing bean action to every row
               </a>
               with the difference that you can introduce colspans to your taste. The example also shows how to use
               <span class="code">
                f:verbatim
               </span>
               whether to render plain vanilla HTML or not. The example also shows how to alternate the row colors using the
               <span class="code">
                c:forEach varStatus
               </span>
               . The
               <span class="code">
                f:setPropertyActionListener
               </span>
               (which was introduced in JSF 1.2 and only works inside
               <span class="code">
                UICommand
               </span>
               components) will set the current
               <span class="code">
                dataItem
               </span>
               object in the appropriate property of the backing bean. It is the same
               <span class="code">
                dataItem
               </span>
               object as you should obtain by
               <span class="code">
                HtmlDataTable#getRowData()
               </span>
               when using a regular
               <span class="code">
                h:dataTable
               </span>
               .
              </p>
              <h5>
               <a href="#top">
                Back to top
               </a>
              </h5>
              <h4>
               <a href="#DownloadWAR" name="DownloadWAR">
                Download WAR
               </a>
              </h4>
              <p>
               Here is a WAR containing all of the above examples in Request as well as Session scope. This WAR also contains "
               <b>
                The ultimate CRUD example
               </b>
               " which is a show-off of the capacities of datatables (and JSF itself).
              </p>
              <p>
               <a href="https://app.box.com/shared/d1rdqp3wwk" target="_blank">
                UsingDatatables.war
               </a>
               <small>
                (1.49 MB, updated at 2008-12-08)
               </small>
               , based on JSF 1.2_10 in a Java EE 5.0 environment.
              </p>
              <p>
               This WAR is developed and tested in
               <a href="http://balusc.blogspot.com/2008/01/jsf-tutorial-with-eclipse-and-tomcat.html">
                Eclipse 3.4 using Tomcat Application Server 6.0.18
               </a>
               .
              </p>
